<title>The term resource management refers to the operations used to control how capabilities provided by Grid resources and services are made available to other entities, whether users, applications, or services. Strictly speaking, resource man-agement is concerned not with the core function of a resource or servicethat is, what it does for clientsbut rather with the manner in which this function is per-formed, such as when a requested operation starts or how long it takes to complete.</title>
